### [1] [Visual Text Compression as Measure Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06708)
*Lv Tang,Tianyi Zheng,Yang Liu,Bo Li,Xingyu Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文提出用测度传输视角刻画“视觉文本压缩（VTC）”的信息损失，并据此实现无标注路由与基于运输成本的再编码（“注视/foveation”），在24个数据集上以更少token取得更高或相当性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VTC通过把文本渲染为图像再由多模态模型编码，能显著减少解码端token，但下游效果起伏很大，且压缩率并不预测任务表现。缺的是能量化“与任务相关的信息损失”的度量，以决定何时走视觉路径，以及如何补救损失。

Method: 将VTC表述为测度传输：把文本token与视觉token视作经验测度，ViT补丁编码器对应一个push-forward映射，其传输成本可分解为两部分：精度成本（patch内聚合导致的信息损失）与覆盖成本（跨patch碎片化导致的信息缺失）。两项成本可用无需下游标签的探针估计。基于该成本：1）提出无标签的路由准则，按输入/实例决定是否采用视觉路径；2）提出“运输感知的注视”机制，对高成本区以更高分辨率重编码。

Result: 在Qwen3-4B上覆盖24个NLP数据集：无标签路由在17/24数据集上与按数据集调参的oracle一致（70.8%）；相较纯LLM基线，平均任务得分+3.3%，平均token数-10.3%。

Conclusion: 测度传输提供了分析VTC信息损失的可操作框架，使得无需标签即可进行路径选择，并用成本指导的局部高分辨率再编码缓解损失，从而在保持或提升任务性能的同时降低token开销。

Abstract: Visual text compression (VTC) promises efficient long-context processing by rendering text into an image and re-encoding it with a vision-language model, often producing $3$--$20\times$ fewer decoder tokens than subword tokenization. Yet token savings do not translate predictably into downstream utility: on some tasks the visual path matches or exceeds the text path, on others it collapses, and the compression ratio itself does not predict which regime will occur. The missing quantity is therefore not another summary of efficiency, but a principled measure of task-relevant information loss induced by visual encoding. We address this problem by formulating VTC in the language of measure transport. Treating text and visual tokens as empirical probability measures, we show that the ViT patch encoder induces a push-forward map whose transport cost decomposes into a precision cost from within-patch aggregation and a coverage cost from cross-patch fragmentation. Both terms are estimable from downstream-label-free probes. This formulation yields two operational consequences: a downstream-label-free routing criterion that selects whether to use the visual path for a given input or benchmark instance, and a transport-informed foveation mechanism that re-encodes high-cost regions at higher resolution. Across $24$ NLP datasets at Qwen3-4B, our label-free rule matches the per-dataset oracle on $17/24$ datasets ($70.8\%$), and improves the average task score by $+3.3\%$ with $-10.3\%$ average tokens relative to a pure-LLM.

</details>


### [2] [Edge Deep Learning in Computer Vision and Medical Diagnostics: A Comprehensive Survey](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06714)
*Yiwen Xu,Tariq M. Khan,Yang Song,Erik Meijering*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该综述聚焦“边缘深度学习”在计算机视觉（尤其医疗诊断）中的最新进展：阐明原理与优势，提出硬件平台新分类，梳理在端侧高效部署DNN的方法，综述应用与成效，并展望挑战与未来方向，为研究与实践提供参考。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 云端推理受带宽、时延、隐私与能耗限制；而传感器与数据源日益下沉到终端。为实现实时、可靠、隐私友好且成本可控的智能感知与决策，需要系统性地总结“边缘+深度学习”的方法、硬件与应用，指导平台与模型的协同优化，推动在医学等高价值场景落地。

Method: 文献综述与分类：1) 概述边缘深度学习的原则与技术优势；2) 基于性能与使用场景提出新的边缘硬件平台分类框架；3) 归纳端侧部署DNN的关键技术（轻量化设计、模型压缩等）；4) 汇总计算机视觉与医疗诊断的代表性应用与案例；5) 分析未来研究方向与采用障碍。

Result: 形成一套面向边缘视觉（尤其医疗）的问题图谱与技术框架：给出可操作的硬件平台选择维度；总结端侧高效化的主流策略与工程取舍；通过现实案例展示边缘部署带来的低时延、隐私保护与可靠性提升。

Conclusion: 边缘深度学习有望重塑视觉与医疗诊断等领域的智能流程。要实现规模化落地需软硬协同：面向场景的硬件选型、轻量化与压缩并举的模型设计、兼顾准确性—时延—能耗—隐私的系统优化，并持续攻克标准化、可维护性与安全合规等挑战。

Abstract: Edge deep learning, a paradigm change reconciling edge computing and deep learning, facilitates real-time decision making attuned to environmental factors through the close integration of computational resources and data sources. Here we provide a comprehensive review of the current state of the art in edge deep learning, focusing on computer vision applications, in particular medical diagnostics. An overview of the foundational principles and technical advantages of edge deep learning is presented, emphasising the capacity of this technology to revolutionise a wide range of domains. Furthermore, we present a novel categorisation of edge hardware platforms based on performance and usage scenarios, facilitating platform selection and operational effectiveness. Following this, we dive into approaches to effectively implement deep neural networks on edge devices, encompassing methods such as lightweight design and model compression. Reviewing practical applications in the fields of computer vision in general and medical diagnostics in particular, we demonstrate the profound impact edge-deployed deep learning models can have in real-life situations. Finally, we provide an analysis of potential future directions and obstacles to the adoption of edge deep learning, with the intention to stimulate further investigations and advancements of intelligent edge deep learning solutions. This survey provides researchers and practitioners with a comprehensive reference shedding light on the critical role deep learning plays in the advancement of edge computing applications.

</details>


### [3] [HumanNet: Scaling Human-centric Video Learning to One Million Hours](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06747)
*Yufan Deng,Daquan Zhou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: HumanNet提出一个百万小时、以人为中心的视频语料，融合第一/第三人称视角与丰富互动标注，为具身智能的表征学习、理解、生成与人机迁移提供可扩展数据基座，并通过消融验证其对VLA训练的价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具身智能受限于缺乏大规模、丰富标注的人类物理交互数据；相比视觉与语言可依赖互联网语料扩展，机器人交互数据获取昂贵且稀缺。作者希望用人类活动视频作为可扩展替代，推动具身基础模型规模化。

Method: 构建HumanNet：约100万小时的人类中心视频库，覆盖第一/第三人称、细粒度活动、人-物体互动、工具使用与长时程行为；提出系统化数据策划范式（人类中心过滤、时间结构化、视角多样性、注释增强），并提供交互中心标注（字幕、动作/运动描述、手与身体信号等）。以受控VLA消融进行首步验证：在固定验证集下，基于Qwen VLM继续训练，比较使用HumanNet取样的1000小时自我中心视频与使用Magic Cobot的100小时真实机器人数据。

Result: 使用HumanNet的1000小时第一人称视频继续训练的模型性能超过使用100小时真实机器人数据继续训练的模型，表明自我中心人类视频在效果与可扩展性上优于等量的机器人数据。

Conclusion: 以人为中心的互联网视频经过系统化策划与丰富标注，可成为具身学习的可扩展数据底座，支持表征学习、活动理解、运动生成及人到机器人的迁移；人类自我中心视频可作为成本更低、规模更大的机器人数据替代路径，促进具身基础模型的扩展。

Abstract: Progress in embodied intelligence increasingly depends on scalable data infrastructure. While vision and language have scaled with internet corpora, learning physical interaction remains constrained by the lack of large, diverse, and richly annotated human activity data. We present HumanNet, a one-million-hour human-centric video corpus that captures how humans interact with the physical world at scale. HumanNet spans both first-person and third-person perspectives and covers fine-grained activities, human-object interactions, tool use, and long-horizon behaviors across diverse real-world environments. Beyond raw video, the dataset provides interaction-centric annotations, including captions, motion descriptions, and hand and body-related signals, enabling motion-aware and interaction-aware learning. Beyond scale, HumanNet introduces a systematic data curation paradigm for embodied learning, where human-centric filtering, temporal structuring, viewpoint diversity, and annotation enrichment are treated as first-class design principles. This design transforms unstructured internet video into a scalable substrate for representation learning, activity understanding, motion generation, and human-to-robot transfer. We conduct a first-step validation on the value of this design through controlled vision-language-action ablation: under a fixed set of validation data, continued training from the Qwen VLM model with 1000 hours of egocentric video drawn from HumanNet surpasses the continued training with 100 hours of real-robot data from Magic Cobot, indicating that egocentric human video could be a scalable and cost-effective substitute for robot data. By building this project, we aim to explore the opportunity to scale embodied foundation models using human-centric videos, rather than relying solely on robot-specific data.

</details>


### [4] [R$^3$L: Reasoning 3D Layouts from Relative Spatial Relations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06758)
*Zhifeng Gu,Yuqi Wang,Bing Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出R^3L框架，提升3D布局生成中的相对空间推理的可靠性与一致性，通过不变分解、想象-修订自一致、以及全局到局部参数化的优化，缓解多跳推理中的参考系误差累积与语义/度量漂移，实验显示更物理可行且语义一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MLLM用于推断相对空间关系，但多跳推理需要多次参考系变换，误差累积导致关系不可靠，现有方法常用事后启发式修补，缺乏系统性与一致性保障。

Method: 1) 不变空间分解：将耦合的关系链打断为在参考系变换下不变的子问题，减少误差传播；2) 一致的空间想象：通过“想象—修订”循环，对生成布局进行自一致检查并迭代修正；3) 支持性空间优化：采用全局到局部的坐标重参数化，缓解姿态优化困难。整体形成提升可靠性的通用管线。

Result: 在多种场景与指令上，R^3L生成的布局更物理可行、语义更一致；分析显示解决由参考系引起的不一致是实现可靠多跳相对空间推理的关键。

Conclusion: R^3L通过结构化分解、自一致想象与重参数化优化，有效抑制多跳推理中的参考系误差累积，显著提升3D布局生成中相对空间推理的可靠性与一致性，并验证了处理参考系不一致的重要性。

Abstract: Relative spatial relations provide a compact representation of spatial structure and are fundamental to relative spatial reasoning in 3D layout generation. Recent works leverage Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) to infer such relations, but the inferred relations are often unreliable and are typically handled with post-hoc heuristics. In this paper, we propose R$^3$L, a general framework that improves the reliability and consistency of relative spatial reasoning for 3D layout generation. Our key motivation is that multi-hop reasoning requires repeated reference-frame transformations, which accumulate errors in inferred relations and lead to semantic and metric drift. To mitigate this, we propose invariant spatial decomposition to break coupled relation chains, and consistent spatial imagination to promote self-consistency through an imagine-and-revise loop. We further introduce supportive spatial optimization to ease pose optimization via global-to-local coordinate re-parameterization. Extensive experiments across diverse scene types and instructions demonstrate that R$^3$L produces more physically feasible and semantically consistent layouts. Notably, our analysis shows that resolving frame-induced inconsistencies is crucial for reliable multi-hop relative spatial reasoning. The code is available at https://github.com/Neal2020GitHub/R3L.

</details>


### [5] [LookWhen? Fast Video Recognition by Learning When, Where, and What to Compute](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06809)
*Ali Salamatian,Anthony Fuller,Pritam Sarkar,James R. Green,Leonid Sigal,Evan Shelhamer*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出LookWhen：通过“选择器-提取器”分解视频识别，只处理最有信息的Top-K时空token，以大幅降低FLOPs且保持/提升精度。在多数据集上实现更优准确率-计算权衡，并在实际吞吐上显著更快。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视频Transformer将视频切分为大量token，计算复杂度随token数超线性增长；但视频时空冗余高，不必等量处理全部token。因此需要一种方法自动决定“何时看、看哪里、看什么”，以在不牺牲准确率的情况下减少计算。

Method: 提出LookWhen框架：1) 选择器（浅层）接收降采样视频，为所有时空token打分并选出Top-K；2) 提取器（深层）仅对被选token进行高容量特征提取，以近似全视频表示。训练上，设计两类预训练监督：a) 选择预训练：用基于最近邻距离的“独特性”分数对token排序，鼓励选择器挑选信息量大的token；b) 提取预训练：从视频教师和图像教师蒸馏，并对逐帧表示归一化，强调学习视频内的变化。模型可用于特征抽取或端到端微调。

Result: 在Kinetics-400、SSv2、Epic-Kitchens、Diving48、Jester、Charades等上，与高效模型和同尺寸强化基线相比，LookWhen在准确率-FLOPs的帕累托前沿上9/12个设置占优，其余3个大致持平；按实际吞吐量计，在等精度下比InternVideo2-B快约6.7倍。

Conclusion: 通过显式学习“何时/何处/何物”来选择计算，LookWhen能以少量token近似全视频表示，实现显著的计算节省而不降精度，具备良好的跨任务泛化与实用效率。

Abstract: Transformers dominate video recognition. They split videos into tokens, and processing them has expensive superlinear computational cost. Yet videos are filled with redundancy, so we can question the need for this expense. We introduce LookWhen, a selector-extractor framework that factorizes video recognition into learning when, where, and what to compute. Our shallow selector gets a scaled-down video and quickly scores all tokens across space-time, while our deep extractor gets the top-K selected tokens to approximate full-video representations without actually processing all the tokens. A key challenge is defining effective supervision for selection and extraction. For selection pre-training, we introduce a score on representations that ranks tokens by uniqueness using a simple nearest-neighbor distance. For extraction pre-training, we distill both a video teacher and an image teacher, for which we normalize its frame-wise representations to learn what changes within videos. Through these strategies, our selector-extractor learns general and efficient representations for feature extraction or fine-tuning to a task. Through experiments on Kinetics-400, SSv2, Epic-Kitchens, Diving48, Jester, and Charades, we show that LookWhen achieves a better accuracy-computation trade-off than efficient models and upgraded baselines of similar size. LookWhen Pareto-dominates in accuracy-FLOPs on 9 of 12 cases (6 tasks x 2 settings) and roughly matches on 3. In accuracy-throughput, measuring time in practice, LookWhen is more efficient still at 6.7x faster than InternVideo2-B at equal accuracy.

</details>


### [6] [Knowledge Transfer Scaling Laws for 3D Medical Imaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06859)
*Ho Hin Lee,Dongna Du,Chu Wang,Yuankai Huo,Shi Gu,James C. Gee,Yifan Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出针对3D医学影像多模态（CT/MRI/PET等）统一自监督预训练的数据混合分配方法，基于可预测的尺度律与跨域不对称迁移，构建“枢纽—孤岛”分配策略，在相同预算下显著优于按数据量采样，并在多下游任务上验证有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 跨模态3D医学影像预训练需混合异质域，但现有混合策略多为启发式且忽视不同域的可扩展性与不对称迁移，导致训练效率与下游性能不佳。作者观察到MAE重构损失与跨域迁移呈可预测的幂律趋势，激发将数据分配正规化为尺度律优化问题，以系统性设计最优混合。

Method: 1) 实证测量不同医学影像域在MAE预训练下的尺度规律（损失随数据/算力的幂律）与跨域迁移增益的幂律关系；2) 建立以这些经验幂律为约束的优化模型，求解在给定训练预算下各域的数据分配；3) 由解中抽取“枢纽—孤岛”结构：枢纽域对他域迁移强，应优先配置；孤岛域迁移弱，需要直接投入；4) 与传统按数据比例采样比较，并在分类、器官/病灶分割等下游任务上验证。

Result: - 发现不同域的可扩展速率不同，跨域知识迁移强烈不对称；- MAE重构损失与跨域迁移均符合可预测的幂律趋势；- 基于迁移感知的分配在预训练阶段较按数据量比例采样最高提升58%，并能在未见预算上泛化（相关系数r=0.989）；- 下游疾病分类与器官/病灶分割任务上，一致获得更强表征与更好性能。

Conclusion: 将数据混合设计为尺度律优化可系统地利用跨域不对称迁移，形成可解释的“枢纽—孤岛”分配；该策略在3D医学影像预训练中优于启发式采样，并能跨预算泛化，提供更强的通用临床表示。

Abstract: Vision foundation models are increasingly moving beyond 2D to volumetric domains such as 3D medical imaging, where unified pretraining across different imaging modalities (i.e. CT, MRI, and PET) could provide foundational models for diverse clinical tasks. However, training such models requires mixing heterogeneous imaging domains, and current mixture strategies remain largely heuristic. In this work, we observe that different medical imaging domains scale at variable rates during pretraining, and knowledge transfer between domains is strongly asymmetric: training on one domain can substantially improve another, but the reverse may be much weaker. Interestingly, both MAE reconstruction loss and cross-domain transfer follow predictable power-law trends with domain-specific behaviors. Motivated by these findings, we formulate data allocation as a scaling-law optimization problem. The derived allocations reveal an interpretable hub-and-island structure: highly transferable domains emerge as hubs that benefit many others and deserve strategic allocation, while isolated domains act as islands requiring direct investment. Empirically, transfer-aware allocation outperforms data-proportional sampling by up to 58% and generalizes well to unseen budgets with r=0.989. Downstream validation on disease classification and organ/lesion segmentation further confirms that the derived transfer-aware mixtures provide stronger pretrained representations for clinical 3D medical imaging tasks.

</details>


### [7] [AdpSplit: Error-Driven Adaptive Splitting for Faster Geometry Discovery in 3D Gaussian Splatting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06876)
*Yongjae Lee,Jingxing Li,Abhay Kumar Yadav,Rama Chellappa,Deliang Fan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出AdpSplit：在3D Gaussian Splatting中用误差驱动的自适应切分替代固定二分，从而以更少的致密化轮次达到同等渲染质量并显著缩短训练时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统3DGS的致密化通过固定基数（二分）随机切分高误差高斯以捕捉细节；但二分需要多轮迭代才能暴露细粒度结构，成为短训练日程（少迭代）下的效率瓶颈。需要一种能更快、针对性更强地增加高斯密度的方法。

Method: 提出AdpSplit：基于L1像素误差统计，按区域误差自适应决定每个父高斯的切分子数，并用误差区域的统计来初始化子高斯参数（位置、尺度、颜色/不透明度等），以误差驱动而非固定二分的方式进行致密化。作为标准split算子的即插即用替换，兼容多种加速3DGS管线（如FastGS）。

Result: 在MipNeRF360、Deep-Blending、Tanks&Temples等数据集上，作为drop-in替换，AdpSplit为多种加速3DGS管线带来约9.2%–22.3%的训练时间降低；结合FastGS，在MipNeRF360上在保持与完整训练日程相当的PSNR的同时减少16.4%训练时间，相对原始3DGS实现12.6×整体加速。

Conclusion: 误差驱动的自适应切分可在不牺牲渲染质量的前提下显著减少致密化轮次与训练时间，并能无缝集成进现有3DGS加速框架，是对固定二分策略的有效替代。

Abstract: Adaptive density control in 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) repeatedly grows the Gaussian population through fixed-cardinality random splitting to discover useful scene structure. However, in vanilla 3DGS, its binary split operator requires many densification rounds to expose fine details, making it a bottleneck for efficient training schedules with fewer iterations. We introduce AdpSplit, an error-driven adaptive split operator that determines the number of split children and initializes the child parameters from L1-pixel-error region statistics, enabling fewer densification iterations, thus reduced training time, while preserving the rendering quality of full-schedule training. Across the MipNeRF360, Deep-Blending, and Tanks&Temples datasets, AdpSplit reduces the training time of multiple accelerated 3DGS pipelines by 9.2%-22.3% as a simple drop-in replacement for the standard split operator. With FastGS, AdpSplit matches the full-schedule PSNR on MipNeRF360 while reducing training time by 16.4%, corresponding to a 12.6x acceleration over vanilla 3DGS.

</details>


### [8] [TriDE: Triangle-Consistent Translation Directions for Global Camera Pose Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06889)
*Francisco Chen,Yiran Wang,Yunpeng Shi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出TriDE，通过三角形一致性与消息传递联合校正成对平移方向，显著提升SfM全局位姿中的方向精度与相机定位效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 成对平移方向常被独立估计，易受噪声/外点影响并与图中其他对不一致，进而削弱全局相机定位的稳定性与精度。需要一种在不进行昂贵且对初值敏感的全局非线性优化下，能联合利用更高阶结构一致性的方向估计方法。

Method: 引入基于相机三角形（camera-triangle）的高阶一致性约束，构建方向与其相邻加权三角形之间的因子图，通过消息传递迭代地下调不可靠的成对方向、上调一致方向的权重，实现方向的联合精炼；避免直接求解全局非线性问题，并给出在随机腐败模型下的精确恢复相变界限。

Result: 在真实图像图上，TriDE显著降低相对方向误差，较基线方法取得更高的方向准确性，并在下游全局相机位置估计中得到更优的重建结果。理论上，给出强相变界限保证在一定腐败率下可精确恢复。

Conclusion: 利用三角形一致性与消息传递，可在无需昂贵全局优化的前提下稳健地联合估计方向，实用地桥接了本地成对估计与全局相机位姿几何之间的鸿沟。

Abstract: Pairwise translation directions are a key input to camera location estimation in global structure-from-motion. Existing estimators usually process each image pair independently, producing directions that may be locally plausible but inconsistent with the other relative directions in the viewing graph. To jointly estimate the direction, we propose TriDE, which exploits camera-triangle consistency as an efficient higher-order verification signal. Instead of solving a costly global nonlinear optimization problem that is sensitive to initialization, TriDE refines unreliable pairwise directions through message passing between directions and their incident weighted triangles. This information propagation strategy enables us to establish a strong phase-transition bound for exact recovery under a realistic random corruption model. Experiments on real image graphs show that TriDE improves direction accuracy by a large margin and yields better downstream camera locations, providing a practical link between local pairwise estimation and global camera pose geometry.

</details>


### [9] [Towards Fairness under Label Bias in Image Segmentation: Impact, Measurement and Mitigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06891)
*Aditya Parikh,Stella Frank,Sneha Das,Aasa Feragen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种针对图像分割的“置信学习”数据中心改编，无需干净真值即可直接在训练数据中检测并缓解群体条件的标签偏差，实现各亚群体更公平的性能。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分割数据集的标注流程会产生群体条件的标签错误（标签偏差），导致不同人群性能差异；现有方法通常需要干净真值来检测偏差，但这在实际中难以获得，因此需要一种无需干净标注即可发现与量化偏差的方法。

Method: 将Confident Learning（CL）思想扩展到分割：用模型在像素/区域级的高置信预测与训练标签比对，识别具有方向性的系统性错误（例如某类被系统性误标为另一类），以此度量偏差；同时分析编码器特征空间中亚群体可分性受偏差影响的现象，并将这种可分性用于偏差缓解，而非仅抑制；在三类数据集（含合成与真实偏差）上进行评估。

Result: 所提框架在无需干净真值的情况下，能稳定检测并量化分割标注中的标签偏差，发现并利用由偏差引起的特征空间可分性；在三个数据集与多种实验条件下，实现对偏差的缓解并使各亚群体性能趋于公平，标准重叠指标（如Dice）难以揭示的方向性错误被成功识别。

Conclusion: 数据中心的CL改编可在无干净标注条件下有效发现与缓解图像分割中的标签偏差，通过利用编码器特征的亚群体可分性，实现更公平的一致性能，优于仅依赖Dice等重叠指标的做法。

Abstract: Labeled datasets reflect the biases of their annotation pipelines, which sometimes introduce label bias: group-conditional label errors that cause systematic performance disparities across demographic subgroups. Label bias in image segmentation remains underexplored, as even detecting it typically requires clean, unbiased annotations, which are not readily available. We present a data-centric adaptation of Confident Learning to segmentation, allowing detection of label bias directly in the training data without a clean, unbiased ground truth. By comparing the provided training labels to the model's confident predictions, we isolate directional errors that quantify the presence and nature of bias, where standard overlap metrics like Dice fail. We further show that label bias influences subgroup separability in the encoder's feature space, an artifact we leverage for bias mitigation rather than suppressing it. We evaluate three datasets, spanning from synthetic to real-life bias, showing how our framework reliably detects and mitigates bias without access to clean labels, achieving equitable performance across experimental conditions.

### [10] [Not All Tokens Need 40 Steps: Heterogeneous Step Allocation in Diffusion Transformers for Efficient Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06892)
*Ernie Chu,Vishal M. Patel*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出HSA：在DiT视频扩散推理中按token运动速度分配异步去噪步数，并用KV缓存同步与一次性缓存Euler更新处理跳过token，显著在相同或更低计算下保持/提升质量，Pareto更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准推理对所有时空token使用相同步数，计算昂贵且与人类视觉对冗余运动的忽略不一致；需要在不牺牲全局上下文的前提下减少无效计算。

Method: 训练无关的异步推理框架HSA：1) 基于token速度动力学为不同时空token分配不同去噪步预算；2) KV-cache同步机制，使活跃token能注意完整序列而跳过不活跃token的计算；3) 推导缓存版Euler更新，对被跳过token的潜变量一次推进，无需额外前向计算。

Result: 在Wan-2与LTX-2上、涵盖T2V与I2V任务，HSA在激进加速（如50%与25%运行时）下相较前沿缓存方法与原生Flow Matching基线，结构保持更稳、质量更高，质量-时延Pareto前沿显著更优且无需离线画像。

Conclusion: HSA能在不改动训练的前提下，以异构步数分配与缓存机制高效推理DiT视频生成，在严苛算力预算下依然保持结构与质量，提供更优质量-效率折中，具有通用与实用价值。

Abstract: Diffusion Transformers (DiTs) have achieved state-of-the-art video generation quality, but they incur immense computational cost because standard inference applies the same number of denoising steps uniformly to every token in the sequence. It is well known that human vision ignores vast amounts of redundant motion. Why, then, do our densest models treat every spatiotemporal token with equal priority? In this paper, we introduce Heterogeneous Step Allocation (HSA), a training-free inference algorithm that assigns varying step budgets to different spatiotemporal tokens based on their velocity dynamics. To resolve the resulting sequence-length mismatch without sacrificing global context, HSA introduces a KV-cache synchronization mechanism that allows active tokens to attend to the full sequence while entirely bypassing inactive tokens. Furthermore, we derive a cached Euler update that advances the latent states of skipped tokens in a single operation without additional model evaluations. We evaluate HSA on the Wan-2 and LTX-2 models for both text-to-video (T2V) and image-to-video (I2V) generation. Our results demonstrate that HSA significantly outperforms previous state-of-the-art caching methods and the vanilla Flow Matching baseline, especially at aggressive acceleration regimes (e.g., 50% and 25% runtimes). Crucially, HSA achieves a superior quality-runtime Pareto frontier without the need for expensive offline profiling, robustly preserving structural integrity and generation quality even under tight computational budgets.
  Project page: https://ernestchu.github.io/hsa

</details>

Abstract: Synthesizing consistent and coherent long video remains a fundamental challenge. Existing methods suffer from semantic drift and narrative collapse over long horizons. We present A$^2$RD, an Agentic Auto-Regressive Diffusion architecture that decouples creative synthesis from consistency enforcement. A$^2$RD formulates long video synthesis as a closed-loop process that synthesizes and self-improves video segment-by-segment through a Retrieve--Synthesize--Refine--Update cycle. It comprises three core components: (i) Multimodal Video Memory that tracks video progression across modalities; (ii) Adaptive Segment Generation that switches among generation modes for natural progression and visual consistency; and (iii) Hierarchical Test-Time Self-Improvement that self-improves each segment at frame and video levels to prevent error propagation. We further introduce LVBench-C, a challenging benchmark with non-linear entity and environment transitions to stress-test long-horizon consistency. Across public and LVBench-C benchmarks spanning one- to ten-minute videos, A$^2$RD outperforms state-of-the-art baselines by up to 30% in consistency and 20% in narrative coherence. Abstract: Infrared-Visible image fusion (IVIF) aims to integrate thermal information and detailed spatial structures into a single fused image to enhance perception. Recent IVIF reward-modelling efforts learn from human ratings but use scalar regression on aggregated scores, neither leveraging the reasoning of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) nor encoding per-image perceptual ambiguity in their supervision, but naively introducing MLLMs with discrete one-hot supervision likewise collapses fused images of similar quality into different rating levels. ### [15] [TRAJGANR: Trajectory-Centric Urban Multimodal Learning via Geospatially Aligned Neural Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06990)

Method: 提出TrajGANR：学习轨迹的连续神经表示，可在路径任意点生成表征，并与附近（不必与轨迹航点同址）的街景图像做细粒度对齐；设计联合对齐三种模态（轨迹、街景图像、地理位置）的MSSL目标；在多任务上进行评估与消融以验证组件作用。

However, existing geospatial MSSL methods are mainly designed for static pairs of modalities, such as satellite imagery, street-view imagery, and text, where learning is driven by aligning observations from the same or nearby locations. This assumption breaks down for human mobility trajectories, which represent continuous movement along paths rather than discrete observations at individual locations. Although trajectories are important for urban understanding through their ability to capture human activity across roads, neighborhoods, and places over time, they remain largely underexplored in current geospatial MSSL frameworks. We present TrajGANR, a novel trajectory-centric geospatial MSSL framework that aligns continuous movement patterns with static, location-based observations. TrajGANR learns a continuous neural representation of trajectories at arbitrary points along each path, which enables fine-grained alignment with nearby street-view images, even when they are not co-located with any trajectory waypoints. We leverage this capability to introduce an MSSL objective that jointly aligns three modalities: trajectories, street-view images, and their geographic locations. We evaluate TrajGANR on four urban mobility and road understanding tasks. Across these tasks, TrajGANR consistently outperforms existing geospatial MSSL frameworks and a trajectory-specific foundation model. Ablation studies further demonstrate that our proposed MSSL objective and the multimodal learning framework are the primary drivers of these improvements, highlighting the importance of fine-grained geospatial alignment over coarser aggregation, as well as geospatial multimodal learning.

*Roy Xie,Dan Friedman,Donghan Yu,Bowen Pan,Christopher Fifty,Jang-Hyun Kim,Xianzhi Du,Zhe Gan,Vivek Rathod,Bhuwan Dhingra*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出LensVLM：在将文本渲染为图像并进行强压缩的场景下，通过“先扫描压缩图，再有选择地放大相关区域”的推理与后训练框架，显著缓解分辨率不足导致的识别退化，取得接近未压缩文本上限的准确率与更高压缩比上的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将文本当作图像输入VLM可避免长文本分词与长序列成本，但随图像压缩（降分辨率）字符会小到难以辨认，准确率急剧下降。需要一种在高压缩下仍能保留任务相关细节、同时控制计算开销的方法。

Method: 提出LensVLM：1) 推理框架：先用VLM在高压缩图像上粗读与定位，借助“学习到的工具”选择性地对与问题相关的局部或整页进行高分辨率扩展（两类工具：文本扩展与高分辨率图像扩展）；2) 后训练配方：训练模型学会何时、如何选择工具与整合扩展内容，使其对渲染选择更鲁棒，并逐步由不可靠的视觉阅读转向依赖扩展内容。

Result: 基于Qwen3.5-9B-Base，LensVLM在七个文本问答基准上实现约4.3倍有效压缩下接近未压缩文本的上限准确率，并在高达10.1倍有效压缩时显著优于基于检索、文本压缩和视觉压缩的强基线；在多模态文档与代码理解任务中同样泛化，且压缩越高领先越明显。

Conclusion: 选择性放大+工具学习能在高压缩下保持乃至提升VLM的理解能力；训练使模型对渲染更鲁棒，并在高压缩时更多依赖扩展内容。实践上：渲染文本优先用文本扩展；原生文档（布局重要）优先用高分辨率图像扩展。

Abstract: Vision Language Models (VLMs) offer the exciting possibility of processing text as rendered images, bypassing the need for tokenizing the text into long token sequences. Since VLM image encoders map fixed-size images to a fixed number of visual tokens, varying rendering resolution provides a fine-grained compression knob. However, accuracy deteriorates quickly as compression increases: characters shrink below the vision encoder's effective resolution, making them indistinguishable. To address this, we propose LensVLM, an inference framework and post-training recipe that enables VLMs to scan compressed images, then selectively expand only the relevant images to their uncompressed form via learned tools. Building on Qwen3.5-9B-Base, LensVLM maintains accuracy comparable to the full-text upper bound at 4.3x effective compression and outperforms retrieval-based, text- and visual-compression baselines up to 10.1x effective compression across seven text QA benchmarks. LensVLM also generalizes to multimodal document and code understanding tasks, with the accuracy gain over baselines growing as compression increases. Our analysis validates this approach: training makes visual compression robust to rendering choices, and as compression grows the model increasingly relies on expanded content rather than unreliable visual reading. The analysis also yields practical tool-choice guidance: text expansion is preferable for rendered text, while high-resolution image expansion suits native documents whose layout cues carry task-relevant information.

</details>


### [17] [OneViewAll: Semantic Prior Guided One-View 6D Pose Estimation for Novel Objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07023)
*Yang Luo,Yan Gong,Yongsheng Gao,Jie Zhao,Xinyu Zhang,Huaping Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: OneViewAll在仅有单个RGB-D参考视图、无CAD模型的条件下，通过“投影-对比”范式与多层次语义先验，实现高效6D位姿估计，在LINEMOD上达92.5% ADD-0.1，显著优于One2Any的52.6%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实应用常仅有一张真实参考图且缺乏CAD，多数方法依赖显式3D模型或多视图，难以扩展；需要一种在单参考、无模型的设定下依旧稳健且高效的位姿估计方法，尤其能处理对称、少纹理与遮挡。

Method: 提出OneViewAll框架：以投影等变空间中的“投影-对比”范式直接对齐参考与查询，无需CAD渲染。分三级整合语义先验：1) 类别/场景级先验用于高效假设初始化；2) 物体级对称先验通过镜像融合实现几何补全；3) Patch级先验进行判别式细化；并保持低推理延迟。

Result: 在LINEMOD上用单个真实参考视图取得92.5% ADD-0.1，显著超过CVPR 2025基线One2Any的52.6%；在YCB-V、Real275、Toyota-Light等数据集上也有一致提升，且推理延迟低；对对称、无纹理、被遮挡物体表现突出。

Conclusion: 语义先验与对称感知的投影-对比策略，可在单参考、无CAD场景下实现强健、可扩展的6D位姿估计，并在多基准上验证其准确与高效。

Abstract: In many practical 6D object pose estimation scenarios, we often have access to only a single real-world RGB-D reference view per object, typically without CAD models. Existing methods largely rely on explicit 3D models or multi-view data, which limits their scalability. To address this challenging single-reference model-free setting, we propose \textbf{OneViewAll}, a semantic-prior-guided framework that performs pose estimation via a novel Project-and-Compare paradigm. Instead of relying on computationally expensive CAD-based rendering, our method directly aligns reference and query observations within a projection-equivariant space. OneViewAll progressively integrates hierarchical semantic priors across three levels: (1) \textit{category- and scene-level} priors for efficient hypothesis initialization; (2) \textit{object-level symmetry} priors for geometry completion via mirror fusion; and (3) \textit{patch-level} priors for discriminative refinement. Extensive experiments demonstrate that OneViewAll achieves \textbf{92.5\%} ADD-0.1 accuracy on the LINEMOD dataset using only one real reference view -- significantly outperforming the CVPR 2025 baseline One2Any (52.6\%). It also yields consistent improvements on YCB-V, Real275, and Toyota-Light while maintaining low inference latency. Our results underscore the efficacy of symmetry-aware projection in handling symmetric, texture-less, and occluded objects.

</details>


### [18] [Pan-FM: A Pan-Organ Foundation Model with Saliency-Guided Masking for Missing Robustness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07055)
*Qiangqiang Wu,Grace McIlvain,Zhou Yu,Junhao Wen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Pan-FM：一个可在“器官缺失”现实场景下进行跨器官学习的全身医学影像基础模型；通过统一骨干+掩码式自蒸馏，并引入显著性引导掩码（SGM）抑制优势器官偏置；在UK Biobank上对多疾病预测与缺失鲁棒性优于单/多器官基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实的人体老化与疾病涉及多器官协同过程，但现有基础模型多为单模态、单域（如仅脑MRI），难以学习全身表征；真实多模态生物医学数据普遍“非随机缺失”（MNAR），导致偏差、泛化差与效能下降，亟需能够处理缺失并实现跨器官学习的FM。

Method: 构建Pan-FM：1）统一骨干网络，可在训练与推理阶段处理器官缺失；2）采用基于掩码的自蒸馏进行预训练；3）发现朴素多器官预训练会产生“优势器官捷径偏置”（脂肪、心脏主导）；为此提出显著性引导掩码（SGM），利用模型注意力分布自适应地更强地掩码优势器官，促进均衡的跨器官学习；SGM计算开销可忽略，易于融入现有自监督框架。

Result: 在UK Biobank数据上，Pan-FM在13类疾病与14个单疾病任务上优于单器官与多器官基线，并在器官缺失设定下表现出更强鲁棒性；表明其能更均衡地学习全身表征并缓解优势器官偏置。

Conclusion: Pan-FM为系统神经科学中的现实模态缺失问题提供可扩展解决方案，推动从单器官向全身、更具泛化性的医学影像基础模型发展；SGM作为轻量模块可广泛提升多器官表征学习。

Abstract: Foundation models (FMs) have shown great promise in medical imaging, but most FMs are trained on unimodal data within isolated domains, such as brain MRI alone. Human aging and disease arise through coordinated biological processes across organs, therefore motivating multimodal FMs that learn whole-body representations. A key challenge, however, is that real-world multimodal biomedical data are often missing not at random, which can reduce power, limit generalizability, and introduce bias. We propose Pan-FM, a pan-organ foundation model pre-trained on imaging from seven organs (Brain, Heart, Adipose, Liver, Kidney, Spleen, and Pancreas) under realistic missing-organ scenarios. Pan-FM uses a unified backbone that handles organ missingness during both training and inference, and is pre-trained with masking-based self-distillation. We find that naive multimodal pre-training leads to dominant-organ shortcut learning bias, with the model over-relying on dominant organs such as adipose and heart. To address this, we introduce Saliency-Guided Masking (SGM), which uses the model attention distribution to adaptively mask dominant organs during pre-training, thus encouraging more balanced cross-organ, whole-body learning. Notably, SGM introduces negligible computational overhead and can be seamlessly integrated into existing self-supervised learning frameworks to improve multi-organ representation learning. On the UK Biobank, Pan-FM achieves stronger prediction across 13 disease categories and 14 single disease entities than single-organ and multi-organ baselines, with improved robustness under missing-organ settings. Pan-FM serves as a scalable solution to realistic modality-missingness in multimodal learning in system neuroscience and as a step toward more generalizable whole-body FMs.

### [19] [Learning to Track Instance from Single Nature Language Description](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07064)
*Yaozong Zheng,Bineng Zhong,Qihua Liang,Shuimu Zeng,Haiying Xia,Shuxiang Song*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种无需边界框标注的自监督视觉-语言跟踪方法，通过动态令牌聚合，让语言引导在视频中持续定位被指称目标，并在多基准上优于现有自监督方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VL跟踪多依赖标注的框监督或简单、均等的视觉-语言融合，导致训练成本高、冗余视觉噪声干扰大、语义对齐弱，难以在无框标注的场景下学到稳健的语言引导跟踪能力。

Method: 提出自监督VL跟踪器“Tracker”（文中符号），核心为动态令牌聚合模块：1) 以模板帧的锚点token为依据，选择多个关键目标视觉token；2) 依据注意力权重融合这些目标token并聚合进语言token，抑制冗余视觉噪声、强化语义对齐；3) 使用融合后的语言token作为引导，在搜索帧中提取潜在目标token，并将其传播到后续帧，形成时间提示，促使模型从无标注视频中自主学习实例级跟踪。

Result: 在多个VL跟踪基准上，所提方法超越现有自监督SOTA；实验表明动态令牌聚合带来显著的鲁棒性与对齐性提升，并能在无框标注下学到有效的语言引导跟踪表征。

Conclusion: 动态、非均质的视觉-语言令牌聚合可在无边界框标注条件下实现强大的自监督语言引导跟踪，减少标注成本并提升跨帧语义一致性与跟踪性能。

Abstract: How to achieve vision-language (VL) tracking using natural language descriptions from a video sequence \textbf{without relying on any bounding-box ground truth}? In this work, we achieve this goal by tackling \textit{self-supervised VL tracking}, which aims to evaluate tracking capabilities guided by natural language descriptions. We introduce \textbf{\tracker}, a novel self-supervised VL tracker that is capable of tracking any referred object by a language description. Unlike traditional methods that equally fuse all language and visual tokens, we propose an efficient Dynamic Token Aggregation Module, which treats each visual token \textbf{unequally}. The module consists of three main steps: i) Based on an anchor token, it selects multiple important target tokens from the template frame. ii) The selected target tokens are merged according to their attention scores and aggregated into the language tokens, thereby eliminating redundant visual token noise and enhancing semantic alignment. iii) Finally, the fused language tokens serve as guiding signals to extract potential target tokens from the search frame and propagate them to subsequent frames, enhancing temporal prompts and encouraging the tracker to autonomously learn instance tracking from unlabeled videos. This new modeling approach enables the effective self-supervised learning of language-guided tracking representations without the need for large-scale bounding box annotations. Extensive experiments on VL tracking benchmarks show that {\tracker} surpasses SOTA self-supervised methods.

### [20] [Decoupling Semantics and Fingerprints: A Universal Representation for AI-Generated Image Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07074)
*Zhiyuan Wang,Yanxiang Chen,Yuanzhi Yao,Yunfeng Diao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出ODP-Net，通过光谱上正交的分解与纯化，显式解耦“通用伪造痕迹”、生成器特指指纹与语义内容，从而在未见架构上显著提升检测泛化（如Stable Diffusion 3）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI图像检测器在未见生成架构上易失效，原因是特征纠缠：通用伪造痕迹与生成器指纹、语义内容被混为一谈，模型过拟合于特指指纹与语义，缺乏可迁移的伪造线索。作者通过频谱分析发现不同生成器指纹分布在互不重叠的频率子空间，可被物理上区分。

Method: 提出ODP-Net，包含三部分：1）实例感知正交分解：将特征投影到互斥子空间（通用伪造痕迹、生成器指纹、语义内容）；2）基于扰动的纯化：跨样本特征注入，迫使检测对语义变化不敏感，保留伪造痕迹；3）流形对齐：缩小域间差异，提升跨架构与跨域泛化。核心依据是频谱上“物理正交性”。

Result: 在未见生成架构（如Stable Diffusion 3）上取得SOTA表现，显示与现有方法相比更强的跨架构泛化能力。

Conclusion: 结构性解耦（将通用伪造痕迹与生成器指纹、语义内容显式分离）是提升AI生成图像检测泛化的关键路径；利用频谱正交性进行分解与纯化可有效避免特征纠缠。

Abstract: Detecting AI-generated images across unseen architectures remains challenging, as existing models often overfit to generator-specific fingerprints and semantic content rather than learning universal forgery traces. We attribute this failure to feature entanglement: detectors learn these factors as a single entangled representation, where universal forgery traces are inextricably confounded with both generator-specific fingerprints and semantic content. Crucially, our spectral analysis reveals that this entanglement is avoidable: distinct generator-specific fingerprints (e.g., GAN stripes vs. Diffusion Model spots) occupy disjoint frequency subspaces and coexist as independent superpositions. Leveraging this physical orthogonality, we propose the Orthogonal Decomposition and Purification Network (ODP-Net) to structurally disentangle these factors. Specifically, ODP-Net employs (1) Instance-aware Orthogonal Decomposition to project features into mutually exclusive subspaces: universal forgery traces, generator-specific fingerprints, and semantic content; (2) Perturbation-based Purification to enforce semantic invariance via cross-sample feature injection; and (3) Manifold Alignment to bridge domain gaps. By explicitly decoupling universal forgery traces from generator-specific fingerprints and semantic content, ODP-Net achieves state-of-the-art performance on unseen architectures (e.g., Stable Diffusion 3), validating that structural disentanglement is key to generalization.

</details>


### [21] [Learning Visual Feature-Based World Models via Residual Latent Action](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07079)
*Xinyu Zhang,Zhengtong Xu,Yutian Tao,Yeping Wang,Yu She,Abdeslam Boularias*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种基于视觉特征的世界模型RLA-WM：用从DINO残差中学到的Residual Latent Action（RLA）作为可预测的潜在动作表征，并用flow matching来预测RLA，较现有特征/视频扩散世界模型更准更快；并据此实现两种机器人学习方法：从无动作视频学习的极简世界动作模型，以及完全在离线视频训练的视觉RL框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 像素级视频生成的世界模型效率低且易幻觉；特征世界模型虽高效，但直接回归高维特征会模糊/坍塌，且在高维空间做生成建模困难。需要一种既稳定可预测、又可高效生成的特征空间建模方法与动作表征。

Method: 1) 发现并构建Residual Latent Action（RLA）：从DINO视觉特征的残差信号中提取潜在动作，证明其可预测、可泛化并编码时间进程。2) 提出RLA-WM：用flow matching对RLA分布进行生成式预测，从当前观测与历史动作预测未来RLA；避免直接回归导致的模糊。3) 将RLA-WM用于两种下游：a) 极简世界动作模型（从无动作演示视频中学习RLA动作）；b) 仅基于离线视频、用视频对齐奖励在世界模型内训练的首个视觉RL框架，无需在线交互或手工奖励。4) 在仿真与真实数据集上评测，并与特征模型和视频扩散模型比较。

Result: RLA可从DINO残差中易学得，具预测性与时间性。RLA-WM在仿真与真实数据上优于SOTA特征世界模型与视频扩散世界模型；相较视频扩散速度快数个数量级。两种基于RLA-WM的机器人学习方法有效提升策略学习。

Conclusion: 用RLA作为潜在动作并以flow matching在特征空间生成式建模，可兼得精度与效率，克服特征回归的模糊/坍塌与视频扩散的高成本；这一范式支持从纯离线视频构建世界模型并进行无在线交互的视觉RL，具有广泛的机器人与视频理解应用潜力。

Abstract: World models predict future transitions from observations and actions. Existing works predominantly focus on image generation only. Visual feature-based world models, on the other hand, predict future visual features instead of raw video pixels, offering a promising alternative that is more efficient and less prone to hallucination. However, current feature-based approaches rely on direct regression, which leads to blurry or collapsed predictions in complex interactions, while generative modeling in high-dimensional feature spaces still remains challenging. In this work, we discover that a new type of latent action representation, which we refer to as *Residual Latent Action* (RLA), can be easily learned from DINO residuals. We also show that RLA is predictive, generalizable, and encodes temporal progression. Building on RLA, we propose *RLA World Model* (RLA-WM), which predicts RLA values via flow matching. RLA-WM outperforms both state-of-the-art feature-based and video-diffusion world models on simulation and real-world datasets, while being orders of magnitude faster than video diffusion. Furthermore, we develop two robot learning techniques that use RLA-WM to improve policy learning. The first one is a minimalist world action model with RLA that learns from actionless demonstration videos. The second one is the first visual RL framework trained entirely inside a world model learned from offline videos only, using a video-aligned reward and no online interactions or handcrafted rewards. Project page: https://mlzxy.github.io/rla-wm

### [22] [ImplantMamba: Long-range Sequential Modeling Mamba For Dental Implant Position Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07082)
*Xinquan Yang,Congmin Wang,Xuguang Li,Yulei Li,Linlin Shen,Yongqiang Deng He Meng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出ImplantMamba：结合CNN与Mamba的混合编码器，并引入坡度耦合预测分支（SCP），在无明显纹理的种植体区通过邻牙全局上下文建模，联合回归位置与倾角，实验优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 种植导板设计中，种植体区域纹理贫乏，AI需依赖邻牙纹理推断位置与倾角，现有方法难以同时捕捉局部解剖与全局上下文且位置与倾角预测常脱耦，造成一致性与解剖合理性不足。

Method: 提出长程序列建模网络ImplantMamba：以CNN提取分层局部特征，Mamba选择性扫描实现全卷积体的全局依赖建模；并设计Slope-Coupled Prediction（SCP）分支，将种植体位置回归与倾角回归显式耦合，约束二者的一致性与解剖可行性；在大规模牙种植数据集上训练与评估。

Result: 在大规模牙种植数据集上，ImplantMamba在位置与倾角预测指标上均超越现有方法，表现更优。

Conclusion: 通过CNN+Mamba的混合编码与SCP耦合回归，模型能有效整合邻牙纹理与全局上下文，提升种植体位置和倾角预测的准确性与一致性，适用于临床导板设计。

Abstract: In the design of surgical guides for implant placement, determining the precise implant position is a critical step. However, the implant region itself is often characterized by a lack of distinctive texture in medical images. Consequently, artificial intelligence (AI) models must infer the correct implant position and angulation (slope) primarily by analyzing the texture of the surrounding teeth, which poses a significant challenge. To address this, we propose ImplantMamba, a network architecture designed for long-range sequential modeling to integrate texture information from adjacent teeth. Our approach explicitly couples the regression of the implant position with its slope. The core of ImplantMamba is a hybrid encoder that combines Convolutional Neural Networks (CNNs) with Mamba layers. This design enables the network to hierarchically extract local anatomical features through CNNs while simultaneously modeling global contextual dependencies across the entire scan volume via Mamba's selective scan operations, leading to a more comprehensive understanding of the implant site. Furthermore, we introduce a Slope-Coupled Prediction Branch (SCP). This branch is designed to connect the prediction of implant position with the slope, ensuring internal consistency and anatomical plausibility by thereby enforcing a coherent relationship between the predicted implant location and its angulation. Extensive experiments on a large-scale dental implant dataset demonstrate that the proposed ImplantMamba achieves superior performance compared to existing methods.

### [23] [Task Relevance Is Not Local Replaceability: A Two-Axis View of Channel Information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07086)
*Houman Safaai,Andrew T. Landau,Celia C. Beron,Yasin Mazloumi,Bernardo L. Sabatini*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出将通道重要性分解为两条独立轴：目标轴（与任务相关性）与本地轴（可被同层同伴替代的程度）。发现本地可替代性比目标相关性更能预测剪枝可移除性，并通过理论与实验证实。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往通道重要性常压缩为单一分数，混淆了“通道对任务的重要性”和“被同层同伴替代的能力”。作者希望澄清这两者的区别，以更好地预测通道在剪枝中的可移除性，并解释为何某些相关性强的通道仍可被安全移除。

Method: 提出“两轴视角”：本地轴度量输入捕获与同伴重叠（local replaceability），目标轴度量任务信息与过剩目标信息（target relevance/excess）。在ResNet-18、VGG-16、MobileNetV2上（CIFAR-100）进行度量、相关性与分组分析；随训练进程跟踪两轴解耦；用高斯线性分析解释通过残差化梯度方向导致的分离；做病灶消融与同伴替换实验，检验本地支持对可移除性的影响；在FLOPs匹配的剪枝协议下比较两轴指标的可预测性；在CIFAR-10、Tiny-ImageNet、ImageNet-100与ConvNeXt-T/ImageNet-100上做压力测试。

Result: 两轴仅弱对齐，训练早期即快速分离；本地轴指标在三种CIFAR-100骨干下更稳定、准确地预测通道可移除性，且在多数据集与架构的压力测试中保持同向结论；同时，VGG-16等架构中基于范数的基线依旧具竞争力。实验证明同伴支持在判断可移除性上超越单纯的输入捕获或任务相关性。

Conclusion: 通道重要性不应以单一排序度量。相较目标相关性，本地可替代性更可靠地指引剪枝中通道的可移除性；剪枝应关注“网络在同伴仍在时是否需要该通道”，而非仅问“该通道对任务说了什么”。

Abstract: Channel importance in vision networks is usually summarized by a single score. That summary hides two different questions: how much a channel is related to the task, and whether its function can be supplied by same-layer peers when the channel is removed. We call the second property local replaceability. We introduce a two-axis view that separates these questions. The local axis measures input capture and peer overlap, while the target axis measures task information and target-excess information. Across ResNet-18, VGG-16, and MobileNetV2 trained on CIFAR-100, the two axes are weakly aligned, induce different channel groupings, and separate rapidly during training despite being strongly coupled at random initialization. A Gaussian linear analysis accounts for how this separation can arise through residualized gradient directions, and lesion plus peer-replacement experiments show that peer support refines removability beyond input capture and task relevance alone. Under the fixed FLOPs-matched pruning protocol, local-axis metrics are more reliable predictors of removability than target-axis metrics across the three CIFAR-100 backbones, with the same direction preserved in stress tests on CIFAR-10, Tiny-ImageNet, ImageNet-100, and a ConvNeXt-T/ImageNet-100 pilot. These findings identify an axis-level distinction rather than a universal ranking of pruning scores: local replaceability is a more reliable guide to removability than target relevance, while norm-based baselines remain competitive in architectures such as VGG-16. Relevance-based scores ask what a channel says about the task; pruning asks whether the network still needs that channel when its peers remain available.

</details>

*Hongyang Zhang,Maonnan Wang,Ziyao Wang,Hongrui Yin,Man OnPun*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出InfoGeo，用信息瓶颈与对象中心表示提升跨视角地理定位在复杂域移与UAV杂乱场景下的鲁棒泛化，显著优于SOTA。

Motivation: 现有CVGL多靠全局特征对齐，易受区域纹理/天气导致的域移影响；UAV视角更宽导致大量细粒度目标和视觉杂讯，现有方法难以稳健泛化。

Method: 引入对象中心学习(OCL)思想，构建信息论框架InfoGeo，将训练视为信息瓶颈优化：1) 最大化跨视角的视图不变信息，通过对齐对象级结构关系实现；2) 最小化视图特定噪声，通过跨视角知识约束抑制无关信号。

Abstract: Cross-view geo-localization (CVGL) is fundamental for precise localization and navigation in GPS-denied environments, aiming to match ground or UAV imagery with satellite views. While existing approaches rely on global feature alignment, they often suffer from substantial domain shifts induced by varying regional textures and weather conditions. This issue becomes even more pronounced in UAV-based scenarios, where the broader perspective inevitably introduces dense, fine-grained objects, creating significant visual clutter. To address this, we draw inspiration from Object-Centric Learning (OCL) and propose InfoGeo, an information-theoretic framework designed to enhance robustness and generalization. InfoGeo reformulates the optimization as an information bottleneck process with two core objectives: (i) maximizing view-invariant information by aligning the object-centric structural relations across views, and (ii) minimizing view-specific noisy signals through cross-view knowledge constraints. Extensive evaluations across diverse benchmarks and challenging scenarios demonstrate that InfoGeo significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods.

Abstract: Skeleton-based human activity recognition has achieved strong empirical performance, yet most existing models remain black boxes and difficult to interpret. In this work, we introduce a neurosymbolic formulation of skeleton-based HAR that reframes action recognition as concept-driven first-order logical reasoning over motion primitives. Our framework bridges representation learning and symbolic inference by grounding first-order logic predicates in learnable spatial and temporal motion concepts. Specifically, we employ a standard spatio-temporal skeleton encoder to extract latent motion representations, which are then mapped to interpretable concept predicates via a spatio-temporal concept decoder that explicitly separates pose-centric and dynamics-centric abstractions. These concept predicates are composed through differentiable first-order logic layers, enabling the model to learn human-readable logical rules that govern action semantics. To impose semantic structure on the learned concepts, we align skeleton representations with LLM-derived descriptions of atomic motion primitives, establishing a shared conceptual space for perception and reasoning. Extensive experiments on NTU RGB+D 60/120 and NW-UCLA demonstrate that our approach achieves competitive recognition performance while providing explicit, interpretable explanations grounded in logical structure. Our results highlight neurosymbolic reasoning as an effective paradigm for interpretable spatio-temporal action understanding. Code: https://github.com/Mr-TalhaIlyas/REASON

Conclusion: Qwen3-VL-Seg以极低额外参数，将MLLM的框级定位提升到像素级分割，无需外部大型分割模型；在开放世界与语言复杂场景中效果与泛化俱佳，同时保留通用多模态能力，提供了实用且可扩展的开放世界指代分割范式。

Abstract: Open-world referring segmentation requires grounding unconstrained language expressions to precise pixel-level regions. Existing multimodal large language models (MLLMs) exhibit strong open-world visual grounding, but their outputs remain limited to sparse bounding-box coordinates and are insufficient for dense visual prediction. Recent MLLM-based segmentation methods either directly predict sparse contour coordinates, struggling to reconstruct continuous object boundaries, or rely on external segmentation foundation models such as the Segment Anything Model (SAM), introducing substantial architectural and deployment overhead. We present Qwen3-VL-Seg, a parameter-efficient framework that treats the MLLM-predicted box as a semantically grounded structural prior and decodes it into pixel-level referring segmentation. ### [28] [TriP: A Triangle Puzzle Approach to Robust Translation Averaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07143)
*Zhekai Fan,Wanze Li,Jinxin Wang,Yunpeng Shi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: TriP提出一种基于三角形的平移平均方法：先从三角形几何推断局部边尺度，再在对数域同步重叠三角形的尺度，恢复全局一致的边长与相机位置；对结构化与对抗性腐败鲁棒，避免塌缩，可并行、可扩展，性能显著优于以往。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统平移平均仅依赖方向，缺乏距离信息，导致病态、对噪声和腐败高度敏感，且易出现解塌缩；现有方法在鲁棒性、可扩展性或理论保证上存在不足。

Method: 1) 以三角形为基本单元，从三角形几何关系估计局部相对边尺度；2) 在对数尺度域对重叠三角形进行尺度同步，获得全局一致的边长；3) 由一致边长恢复相机位置。利用三角形的高阶一致性对抗对抗性、循环一致但被破坏的观测等结构化腐败；对数同步天然排除零尺度，从而避免塌缩。算法全并行、计算高效，可扩展到百万级相机图。

Result: 在合成与真实数据集上，TriP在精度与鲁棒性上大幅优于所有现有平移平均方法；在大规模图上保持高效与可扩展性。

Conclusion: 利用三角形高阶一致性与对数尺度同步可实现鲁棒且可扩展的平移平均，理论上可精确恢复位置并在实践中显著超越现有方法，同时天然避免塌缩问题。

Abstract: Translation averaging aims to recover camera locations from pairwise relative translation directions and is a fundamental component of global Structure-from-Motion pipelines. The problem is challenging because direction measurements contain no distance information, making the estimation problem highly ill-conditioned and highly sensitive to corrupted observations. In this paper, we propose TriP, a triangle-based framework for robust translation averaging. TriP first infers local relative edge scales from triangle geometry, and then synchronizes the scales of overlapping triangles in the logarithmic domain to recover globally consistent edge lengths and camera locations. By leveraging higher-order consistency across triangles, the proposed method is robust to adversarial, cycle-consistent, and other structured corruptions. In addition, TriP avoids the collapse issue without requiring any extra anti-collapse constraints, since log-scale synchronization excludes the degenerate zero-scale solution by construction. These structural advantages enable a particularly strong theory for exact location recovery. On the practical side, TriP is fully parallelizable, computationally efficient, and naturally scalable to graphs with millions of cameras. Moreover, it outperforms all previous translation averaging methods by a large margin on both synthetic and real datasets.

Abstract: Underwater salient object detection (USOD) plays a vital role in marine vision tasks but remains fundamentally challenging due to severe visual degradation, such as selective absorption and medium scattering. Conventional pipelines typically adopt a sequential "enhance-then-detect" paradigm. However, isolating low-level visual restoration from high-level semantic perception often leads to semantic inconsistency, where the restored images may not be optimal for detection and can even introduce task-irrelevant noise. To break this sequential bottleneck, we propose UniV2D, a Unified Vision-to-Detection Network that jointly optimizes visual restoration and salient object detection within a mutually beneficial framework. Unlike traditional methods that rely on disjointed pipelines or rigid physical priors, UniV2D introduces a semantic-driven learning paradigm: high-level saliency semantics actively guide the restoration process, while the restored visual cues reciprocally enhance saliency perception. Specifically, UniV2D features a hierarchical dual-branch architecture. It first employs a self-calibrated decoder to predict initial saliency masks alongside a mask-aware restoration module to reconstruct image content. Subsequently, a saliency-guided refinement module equipped with cross-level modulation is utilized to align structural fidelity with semantic consistency. Extensive experiments across multiple benchmarks demonstrate that UniV2D significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods in both quantitative and qualitative evaluations, establishing a new standard for joint underwater perception.

### [30] [Uncovering and Shaping the Latent Representation of 3D Scene Topology in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07148)
*Haoming Wang,Wei Gao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文发现现有VLM内部潜藏可表征三维场景拓扑的“空间子空间”，但被颜色/形状等非几何语义淹没；通过线性特征提取与几何正则（Dirichlet能量）进行潜表示塑形，可显著提升空间推理表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 认知科学表明人类用保拓扑的认知地图在3D中导航；VLM虽能做一定空间推理，但未知其是否具备类似3D内部表征。作者想验证VLM是否含隐式拓扑地图，并寻求方法将其显性化与增强，以提升真实世界空间任务性能。

Method: 1) 通过跨场景的线性特征投影，分离VLM表征中的空间子空间，并用因果干预检验其对空间输出的控制力；2) 从理论上刻画该子空间与场景3D高斯核图的Laplacian特征映射一致，在连续极限收敛至物理3D；3) 基于上述几何识别，引入以Dirichlet能量为核心的潜空间正则化，并在仅500步的SFT上训练，使用简化的合成数据进行塑形。

Result: 提取的空间子空间能因果性地决定模型的空间判断；理论上与Laplacian eigenmaps对应；加入单项Dirichlet正则并做最小量SFT，在真实世界空间基准上显著提升，对涉及场景拓扑理解的任务相比常规SFT和强基线最高提升12.1%。

Conclusion: 当前VLM内部确有可与3D拓扑相对应的潜在空间结构，但被非几何语义干扰。通过线性提取与基于Dirichlet能量的潜空间正则，可对该结构进行数学化塑形，从而高效、低样本地提升VLM的空间拓扑理解能力；方法简单、可泛化，代码已开源。

Abstract: Decades of cognitive science establish that humans navigate environments by forming cognitive maps, defined as allocentric and topology-preserving representations of 3D space. While modern Vision-Language Models (VLMs) demonstrate emergent spatial reasoning from 2D egocentric inputs, it remains unclear whether they construct an analogous 3D internal representation. In this paper, we demonstrate that current VLMs do possess a latent topological map of 3D scenes, but it is heavily overshadowed by non-geometric visual semantics, such as color and shape. By isolating this spatial subspace through cross-scene linear feature extraction, we extract a clean spatial subspace that causally controls the model's spatial outputs. We mathematically shape this latent representation and prove its correspondence to the Laplacian eigenmaps of the scene's 3D Gaussian-kernel graph, converging to the physical 3D space in the continuous limit. Motivated by this geometric identification, we further introduce a mathematically principled latent regularization method for VLMs, based on Dirichlet energy. Applying this single-term regularizer to a minimal 500-step supervised VLM fine-tuning (SFT) on simple synthetic data yields significant improvements on real-world spatial benchmarks, outperforming standard SFT and competitive baselines by up to 12.1\% in spatial tasks involving scene topology understanding. Source code is available at https://github.com/pittisl/vlm-latent-shaping

### [31] [Real-IAD MVN: A Multi-View Normal Vector Dataset and Benchmark for High-Fidelity Industrial Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07149)
*Wenbing Zhu,Jianing Liang,Linjie Cheng,Yurui Pan,Zhuhao Chen,Qingwang Yan,Yudong Cheng,Jianghui Zhang,Mingmin Chi,Bo Peng*

TL;DR: 提出Real-IAD-MVN数据集：用多视角高保真法向图替代稀疏点云，显著提升工业微小几何缺陷检测；并给出跨模态统一原型的重建式基线，优于现有多模态融合方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有IAD方法用2D图像易受纹理/光照影响，难捕捉细微几何缺陷；3D点云虽有形状信息但过于稀疏，无法发现划痕、凹坑等微缺陷。需要既具备微观几何细节、又能覆盖遮挡与侧壁的高密度几何表征与基准。

Method: 构建Real-IAD-MVN：从五个视角采集高保真表面法向图，取代稀疏点云，形成致密“伪3D”多视几何表征；并提出基线：重建式学习框架，从图像与法向图双流中提取跨模态统一原型，以重建误差/特征差异用于异常检测。

Result: 实验证明：多视角致密法向图显著优于稀疏点云用于几何异常检测；所提统一原型重建基线超过现有SOTA多模态融合方法。

Conclusion: 多视高密度法向图能在工业场景中显式揭示侧壁与遮挡处微小缺陷，替代点云成为更有效的几何表征；统一原型跨模态学习提供强基线，数据集为推进几何异常检测奠定基础。

Abstract: Industrial Anomaly Detection (IAD) is critical for quality control, but existing methods struggle with subtle, geometric defects. Standard 2D (RGB) images are sensitive to texture and lighting but often miss fine geometric anomalies. While 3D point clouds capture macro-shape, they are typically too sparse to detect micro-defects like scratches or pits. We address this fundamental data limitation by introducing Real-IAD-MVN (Multi-View Normal), a large-scale industrial dataset. By upgrading our acquisition system, Real-IAD-MVN captures high-fidelity surface normal maps from five distinct viewpoints, replacing sparse 3D data entirely. This provides a comprehensive geometric representation at a micro-detail level, making previously invisible side-wall and occluded defects explicitly detectable. Our experiments, conducted on this new dataset, first provide evidence that incorporating dense, multi-view pseudo-3D (surface normals) yields significantly better detection performance than using sparse 3D point cloud data. To further validate the dataset and provide a strong benchmark, we introduce a baseline method based on reconstruction, which learns to extract cross-modal unified prototypes from the image and normal map streams. We demonstrate that this unified prototype approach surpasses existing state-of-the-art multimodal fusion methods, highlighting the rich potential of our new dataset for advancing geometric anomaly detection.

### [32] [DPG-CD: Depth-Prior-Guided Cross-Modal Joint 2D-3D Change Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07151)
*Luqi Zhang,Zhen Dong,Bisheng Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DPG-CD框架：用影像估计深度作为先验，配合门控融合与多阶段跨时空跨模态特征融合，同时进行2D语义与3D高度变化检测，并辅以DSM重建辅助任务；在Hi-BCD、3DCD及新建NYC-MMCD上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 城市形态演化包含平面扩张与垂直高度变化。现实中3D数据（DSM）更新昂贵且不频繁，但灾害评估与应急需要高频监测。利用事前DSM与事后影像的跨模态、跨时相组合可行，却存在光谱—几何表征鸿沟与“模态差异被误判为变化”的难题，需要稳健融合2D语义与3D几何信息。

Method: 提出DPG-CD：先从影像估计深度作为“深度先验”，缩小与DSM的模态差。通过门控融合有选择地引入几何线索而保留区分性的光谱特征；采用多阶段的跨时相+跨模态特征融合，抽取对变化更敏感的表征；以多任务解码器联合预测2D语义变化与3D高度变化，并加入辅助DSM预测以强化结构一致性和高度估计精度。

Result: 在Hi-BCD、3DCD与新构建的NYC-MMCD三个数据集上，2D与3D变化检测均优于当前SOTA（具体指标未给出，但整体性能领先）。

Conclusion: 深度先验引导与门控融合能有效缩小影像与DSM的模态差，结合跨时相跨模态特征融合与多任务学习，可同时提升2D语义与3D高度变化检测精度，适用于高频城市监测与应急响应。

Abstract: Urban spatial evolution is manifested not only through horizontal expansion but also through vertical structural changes. Consequently, jointly capturing 2D semantic changes and 3D height changes is essential for urban morphology analysis and emergency management. In practical scenarios, collecting 3D observations is often constrained by high acquisition costs and the inability to support frequent updates. The multi-temporal cross-modal input consisting of pre-event Digital Surface Model (DSM) and post-event imagery provides a practical solution for 3D change detection in high-frequency urban monitoring, disaster assessment, and emergency response scenarios. However, this setting remains challenging as imagery and DSM data exhibit significant spectral-geometric representation gaps. Moreover, modality differences may be confused with actual changes, and robust change detection requires effective fusion of semantic and geometric features from multi-temporal data. In this paper, we propose DPG-CD, a depth-prior-guided multi-temporal cross-modal fusion framework for joint 2D semantic and 3D height change detection. Specifically, an estimated depth prior is introduced into the imagery to mitigate the modality gap with DSM. A gated fusion mechanism then selectively injects geometric cues from depth prior while preserving discriminative spectral representations. Subsequently, a multi-stage cross-temporal cross-modal feature fusion architecture is employed to extract change-aware features. Finally, a multi-task decoder jointly predicts 2D semantic changes and 3D height changes, complemented by an auxiliary DSM prediction task to improve structural consistency and height estimation accuracy. Experiments on two public datasets, Hi-BCD and 3DCD, and a new dataset, NYC-MMCD, demonstrate that DPG-CD outperforms state-of-the-art methods on both 2D and 3D change detection tasks.

### [33] [PRIMED: Adaptive Modality Suppression for Referring Audio-Visual Segmentation via Biased Competition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07154)
*Yuchen He,Jing Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出PRIMED方法，用先验解码器判断语句主要依赖的模态（音频/视觉/交互），结合令牌蒸馏与竞争感知跨模态融合，并配合空间感知对齐损失，实现对无关模态的自适应抑制，在Ref-AVS基准上达SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Ref-AVS方法通常将多模态线索同质化融合或提示/推理，难以应对不同场景与指代表达中模态相关性差异，导致受无关或误导模态干扰。需要一种能根据语言与场景自适应调节模态权重、强化前景判别的机制。

Method: 1) 模态先验解码器：根据指代表达预测主要依赖的模态（音频、视觉或其交互），生成模态先验以引导高层注意力并自适应抑制无关模态；2) 令牌蒸馏：从高层视觉特征中提取紧凑的全局视觉token，跨层共享，为多级融合提供层级化全局上下文；3) 竞争感知跨模态融合：在共享全局token的条件下进行跨模态竞争式融合，实现由语言先验调制的注意力分配；4) 空间感知语义对齐损失：引入对比学习以增强前景-背景区分与空间语义对齐。

Result: 在Ref-AVS基准上取得最优总体性能（SOTA），相较现有方法在分割精度与鲁棒性方面均有显著提升。

Conclusion: 通过显式建模视觉知觉与语言驱动的先验调制，并引入自适应模态抑制与层级全局上下文，PRIMED有效缓解无关模态干扰，提升了Ref-AVS的定位与分割表现，具备普适的多模态融合与对齐价值。

Abstract: Referring Audio-Visual Segmentation (Ref-AVS) seeks to localize and segment target objects in video frames based on visual, auditory, and textual referring cues. The task is challenging because the relevance of different modalities varies across referring expressions and scenes, while existing methods typically treat multimodal cues as homogeneous inputs for fusion, prompting, or reasoning, making them vulnerable to irrelevant or misleading modalities. To address this problem, we propose PRIMED, inspired by the biased competition theory in cognitive neuroscience, which explicitly models both visual perception and language-driven prior modulation, and enables more accurate Ref-AVS by adaptive modality suppression. Specifically, a Modality Prior Decoder first estimates whether the referring expression relies primarily on audio, vision, or their joint interaction, generating a modality prior to adaptively guide high-level attention. A Token Distiller further extracts compact global visual tokens from high-level features and shares them across Competition-aware Cross-modal Fusion modules to provide hierarchical global context. Additionally, we introduce a Spatial-Aware Semantic Alignment loss to further enhance foreground-background discrimination through contrastive learning. Extensive experiments on the Ref-AVS benchmark demonstrate that PRIMED achieves state-of-the-art overall performance.

### [34] [Hierarchical Perfusion Graphs for Tumor Heterogeneity Modeling in Glioma Molecular Subtyping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07156)

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出HiPerfGNN：先用VQ‑VAE从DSC‑MRI时序曲线学习量化灌注代码，构建层级图（功能“栖息地”到结构引导的亚区），再用层级GNN跨尺度传播信息以预测IDH、1p/19q与分级；在内部与外部队列上取得高AUC并显示生物学一致的显著性图，证明灌注动力学融入放射基因组学可提升分子分型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有胶质瘤分子分型（IDH、1p/19q）依赖侵入性取样；仅用结构MRI的深度学习难以捕捉区分分型的血流动力学特征。DSC‑MRI具潜力但受多中心差异与逐体素分析局限影响，阻碍临床转化。需要一种稳健、可泛化的方法，将灌注动力学以更高层次表征并跨尺度整合到分型模型中。

Method: 1) 从原始DSC‑MRI时间‑强度曲线用VQ‑VAE学习离散“灌注代码”，将相似血流动力学聚类为功能栖息地，作为图的粗层节点；2) 结合结构MRI，将每个粗层节点分割为细层亚区，形成层级图；3) 采用层级GNN在粗细层之间传播信息并进行分子预测；4) 用内部队列(n=475)训练评估，对外部独立队列(n=397)直接测试；5) 用梯度显著性分析验证生物学合理性。

Result: 内部队列AUC：IDH 0.96、1p/19q 0.89、WHO分级 0.84；外部队列在未重校准情况下IDH AUC 0.89；显著性图与已知胶质瘤病理生理关注模式一致。

Conclusion: 结合DSC‑MRI灌注动力学与层级图学习能稳健提升胶质瘤分子分型的非侵入性预测，并在跨中心数据上保持良好泛化，支持其作为结构MRI的有力补充，具备临床转化潜力。

Abstract: Precise molecular subtyping of gliomas, including isocitrate dehydrogenase (IDH) mutation and 1p/19q codeletion, directly guides surgical and therapeutic decisions, yet currently relies on invasive tissue sampling. Deep learning on structural MRI has emerged as a non-invasive alternative, but anatomy-only approaches cannot capture the hemodynamic signatures that distinguish molecular subtypes. Radiogenomics based on dynamic susceptibility contrast (DSC) MRI holds immense potential for non-invasively characterizing glioma molecular subtypes, yet clinical deployment has been hindered by inter-site variability and the limitations of voxel-wise analysis. We introduce HiPerfGNN, a framework that first learns discrete hemodynamic representations from raw time-intensity curves using a vector-quantized variational autoencoder (VQ-VAE). These quantized perfusion codes define coarse-level graph nodes representing functional tumor habitats, each of which is hierarchically subdivided into fine-level subregions guided by structural MRI. A hierarchical graph neural network then propagates information across scales for molecular prediction. On an internal cohort (n=475), the model achieved AUCs of 0.96 (IDH), 0.89 (1p/19q), and 0.84 (WHO grade), and maintained robust IDH performance (AUC 0.89) on an independent external cohort (n=397) without recalibration. Gradient-based saliency analysis confirms biologically grounded attention patterns aligned with known glioma pathophysiology. Our results demonstrate the added value of integrating perfusion dynamics into radiogenomic pipelines for glioma molecular subtyping. Code is available at https://github.com/janghana/HiPerfGNN.

### [35] [Masks Can Talk: Extracting Structured Text Information from Single-Modal Images for Remote Sensing Change Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07178)
*Kai Zheng,Hang-Cheng Dong,Jiatong Pan,Zhenkai Wu,Fupeng Wei,Wei Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出S2M：从变化检测掩码自动生成结构化文本监督（where/what/how/how many），以零额外标注成本实现精细语义对齐；采用两阶段训练与双向对比学习，在新建的Gaza-Change-v2多类别变化数据集上显著优于现有多模态方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单模态方法常把外观相似但语义无关的变化误判为真实变化；现有多模态方法用文本作辅助但文本要么语义粗糙非结构化，要么由模型生成噪声大。此外被忽视的是：精细变化语义其实已隐含在标准数据集的掩码标签中。

Method: 从变化掩码中自动转写语义四元组（where、what、how、how many），利用固定模板生成多条精确、稠密、无噪声的文本描述作为监督；先进行遥感域特定表征的视觉预训练/微调，再引入多模态解码器与双向对比损失，实现视觉与结构化文本嵌入的深度对齐；构建Gaza-Change-v2多类别变化数据集用于验证。

Result: 在Gaza-Change-v2上取得Sek 17.80%与F_scd 66.14%，超越含大语言模型的多模态基线。

Conclusion: 掩码“会说话”：可在零额外标注成本下提供精细变化语义，结构化文本+双向对比对齐显著提升多类别变化检测性能。

Abstract: Remote sensing change detection is pivotal for urban monitoring, disaster assessment, and environmental resource management. Yet, unimodal deep learning methods frequently confuse genuine semantic changes with visually similar but irrelevant variations. Recent multimodal approaches incorporate text as auxiliary supervision, but their descriptions are either semantically coarse and unstructured or model-generated and thus noisy. Critically, all of them overlook a simple fact: fine-grained change semantics are already implicitly encoded in the ground-truth mask labels that come standard with every change detection dataset. These masks know where the change happened, what the land-cover types were before and after, how the transition occurred, and how many objects were involved. In this paper, we propose S2M, a framework that obtains structured textual features directly from change labels at zero additional annotation cost. Specifically, each change region is automatically transcribed into a semantic quadruple (where, what, how, how many) and converted into several fixed-template text descriptions, providing precise, dense, and noise-free multimodal supervision. We adopts a two-stage training strategy to fine-tune on remote sensing imagery firstly for robust domain-specific representation, after which a multimodal decoder with a bi-directional contrastive loss is introduced to achieve deep alignment between visual features and structured textual embeddings. To validate our method, we construct Gaza-Change-v2, a new multi-class change detection (MCD) dataset about the Gaza Strip. On this MCD dataset, S2M achieves a Sek of 17.80\% and an F$_{\text{scd}}$ of 66.14\%, notably surpassing even multimodal methods that leverage large language models. Our work demonstrates that masks can indeed talk. They tell us exactly what, where, how, and how many changes have occurred.

</details>


### [36] [SatSurfGS: Generalizable 2D Gaussian Splatting for Sparse-View Satellite Surface Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07181)
*Min Chen,Wei Guo,Bin Wang,Wen Li,Tong Fang,Jinbo Zhang,Junqi Zhao,Hong Kuang,Han Hu,Xuming Ge,Qing Zhu,Bo Xu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SatSurfGS提出一种面向稀疏视角卫星影像的可泛化2D高斯铺展(2DGS)表面重建方法，通过置信感知特征融合、跨阶段自一致残差引导和置信双向路由损失，显式建模局部几何可靠性，在渲染质量、重建精度、跨数据集泛化和推理效率上优于通用基线与按场景优化方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 卫星成像多视匹配在大光度差、弱/重复纹理下空间异质性强、约束稀疏且不可靠，导致稀疏视角表面重建困难。现有3DGS不如2DGS适于连续表面表示，但缺乏可泛化、前馈的2DGS框架以稳健处理卫星场景的不均匀几何可靠性。

Method: 构建基于2DGS的由粗到细高斯属性预测框架，并在特征学习、高斯参数估计、训练优化三层面显式建模局部几何置信度：1) 置信感知的单目-多视特征融合，自适应融合单目先验与多视匹配特征；2) 跨阶段自一致残差引导，利用前一阶段渲染高程与当前阶段MVS高程的残差及置信度稳定高斯参数细化；3) 置信双向路由损失，根据局部可靠性在几何与外观监督间进行差异化分配。

Result: 在多个卫星数据集上，相比代表性可泛化基线与竞争性的逐场景优化方法，实现更高的渲染质量、更准的表面/高程重建、更强的跨数据集泛化与更高的推理效率。

Conclusion: 通过在2DGS框架中显式建模局部几何可靠性并进行粗到细的参数预测，SatSurfGS有效缓解稀疏视角卫星影像的匹配不稳定与不均匀性问题，成为兼具精度、泛化与效率的表面重建方案。

Abstract: Sparse-view satellite image surface reconstruction remains highly challenging, fundamentally because the reliability of multi-view matching under satellite imaging conditions is strongly spatially heterogeneous. Affected by large photometric differences, weak textures, and repetitive textures, multi-view geometric constraints are often sparse, unevenly distributed, and locally unreliable. Although 2D Gaussian Splatting (2DGS) is more suitable than 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) for the explicit representation of continuous surfaces, research on generalizable feed-forward 2DGS frameworks for sparse-view satellite surface reconstruction is still lacking. To address this issue, we propose SatSurfGS, a generalizable sparse-view surface reconstruction method for satellite imagery based on 2DGS. The proposed method builds a coarse-to-fine Gaussian attribute prediction framework and explicitly models local geometric reliability at three levels: feature learning, Gaussian parameter estimation, and training optimization. Specifically, we propose a confidence-aware monocular multi-view feature fusion module to adaptively integrate monocular priors and multi-view matching features according to local confidence; a cross-stage self-consistency residual guidance module to stabilize stage-wise Gaussian parameter refinement using the residual between the rendered height map from the previous stage and the current-stage MVS height map, together with confidence information; and a confidence bidirectional routing loss to achieve differentiated allocation of geometric and appearance supervision. Experiments on satellite datasets show that the proposed method achieves improved rendering quality, surface reconstruction accuracy, cross-dataset generalization, and inference efficiency compared with representative generalizable baselines and competitive per-scene optimization methods.

In addition, we introduce a large-scale multi-view near-eye dataset containing comprehensive 2D and 3D annotations under diverse conditions, including train, test, rewear-test, and calibration sessions. Extensive experiments demonstrate that PicoEyes achieves state-ofthe-art performance, consistently outperforming both academic and industrial gaze tracking methods across nocalibration, calibration, rewear-after-calibration, and forecasting settings. ### [38] [Attention Transfer Is Not Universally Effective for Vision Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07191)
*Huaiyuan Qin,Muli Yang,Gabriel James Goenawan,Peng Hu,Chen Gong,Xi Peng,Hongyuan Zhu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文重新评估“仅用注意力迁移即可复现教师ViT预训练收益”的结论，发现并不普适：11个ViT家族中7个成功、4个失败，失败可比无迁移从零训练还差5.1%。失败源于教师与学生的架构不匹配；当给学生加入教师的原生架构组件（随机初始化）后，注意力迁移立刻奏效，而这些组件本身并不提升从零训练表现。结论：注意力足够成立的前提是学生架构需匹配教师。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作声称仅迁移注意力模式即可等效于完整权重迁移，若成立将极大简化知识蒸馏/迁移学习流程。作者动机是验证这一结论在更广泛ViT家族与设置下的稳健性，并定位失败机制。

Method: - 构建覆盖20个教师、11个ViT家族的基准；学生为标准ViT，从随机初始化出发，仅用注意力迁移损失匹配教师注意力。
- 系统评测：不同模型规模、训练时长、迁移数据集、OOD测试。
- 受控分析：拆分注意力通道（如路由/加权）、检查是否能匹配模式及其功能性。
- 架构插拔实验：向学生加入教师的原生架构组件（随机初始化），检验是否恢复迁移有效性。
- 排除项：更换迁移损失、对齐或不对齐预训练配方等。

Result: - 7个家族迁移成功；4个家族在所有规模与设置下稳定失败，最差比无迁移从零训练低5.1%。
- 失败跨规模、一致且在延长训练、换数据、OOD上依旧存在。
- 失败定位到注意力路由通道：学生可匹配模式，但这些模式对学生并不“可用”。
- 在学生中加入教师的原生架构组件（保持随机初始化）即可完全扭转4个家族的失败；这些组件单独对从零训练无益。

Conclusion: “仅靠注意力即可”的命题并非普适；其成立的关键条件是学生与教师的架构匹配。失败并非因损失设计或预训练差异，而是架构不兼容导致学生无法将匹配到的注意力模式转化为功能性表征。

Abstract: A recent work shows that Attention Transfer, which transfers only the attention patterns from a pre-trained teacher Vision Transformer (ViT) to a randomly initialized standard student ViT, is sufficient to recover the full benefit of the teacher's pre-trained weights. We revisit this finding on a comprehensive benchmark of 20 teachers from 11 well-known ViT families and reveal that Attention Transfer is not universally effective. While 7 families transfer successfully, 4 consistently fail, falling up to 5.1\% below the from-scratch no-transfer baseline. Further results demonstrate that this failure is family-consistent across model sizes, and persists under extended training durations, different transfer datasets, and out-of-distribution evaluations. Controlled analyses then consistently localize the problem to the attention-routing channel, indicating that the key issue is not whether the student can match the teacher's attention patterns, but whether the matched patterns remain functional for the student. Crucially, we identify architectural mismatch between the pre-trained teacher and the standard student as the primary mechanism. By adding only the teacher's native architectural components to the student in a randomly initialized state, we completely reverse the failure for all 4 families. Notably, these components alone do not improve from-scratch training, confirming that they specifically unlock the usability of the teacher's attention. We further systematically show that this failure is not explained by the inadequate choice of transfer loss or by differences in pre-training recipes. Our findings refine the prevailing understanding of attention in ViT representations: attention is sufficient \textit{only} when the student architecture matches the teacher.

</details>

Motivation: 传统3DGS/NeRF对重度运动模糊极其脆弱；现有事件相机辅助方法多依赖低分辨率、严格同步与专用硬件，不适合手机等常见设备的手持采集。需要一种既能处理严重模糊、又具高分辨率且无需严格同步的实用方案。

Conclusion: 异步高分辨率RGB-事件系统结合跨域位姿估计与新型损失/正则，可在强模糊下实现稳定高保真的3D重建，具备在常见设备上的实用性，并为社区提供高分数据集促进研究。

Abstract: 3D reconstruction methods such as 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) and Neural Radiance Fields (NeRF) achieve impressive photorealism but fail when input images suffer from severe motion blur. While event cameras provide high-temporal-resolution motion cues, existing event-assisted approaches rely on low-resolution sensors and strict synchronization, limiting their practicality for handheld 3D capture on common devices, such as smartphones. We introduce a flexible, high-resolution asynchronous RGB-Event dual-camera system and a corresponding reconstruction framework. Our approach first reconstructs sharp images from the event data and then employs a cross-domain pose estimation module based on the Visual Geometry Transformer (VGGT) to obtain robust initialization for 3DGS. During optimization, we employ a structure-driven event loss and view-specific consistency regularizers to mitigate the ill-posed behavior of traditional event losses and deblurring losses, ensuring both stable and high-fidelity reconstruction. We further contribute AsyncEv-Deblur, a new high-resolution RGB-Event dataset captured with our asynchronous system. Experiments demonstrate that our method achieves state-of-the-art performance on both our challenging dataset and existing benchmarks, substantially improving reconstruction robustness under severe motion blur. Project page: https://openimaginglab.github.io/AsyncEvGS/

### [40] [Closed-Form Linear-Probe Dataset Distillation for Pre-trained Vision Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07194)
*Bincheng Peng,Guang Li,Ping Liu,Takahiro Ogawa,Miki Haseyama*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出CLP-DD：在冻结特征+线性探针设定下，用闭式求解线性分类器并据此蒸馏数据，显著提升效率与精度，接近或超越现有方法（LGM+DSA），同时更快更省显存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据蒸馏多面向从零训练或需展开长轨迹（LGM）/依赖NTK近似的闭式法，未利用线性探针在冻结特征下可直接闭式解这一关键性质，导致计算昂贵、近似偏差或内环复杂。

Method: 提出闭式线性探针数据蒸馏（CLP-DD）：内层用样本空间的核岭回归（由预训练特征诱导）对合成集求得线性分类器的闭式解；外层不用传统MSE，而用温度缩放的softmax交叉熵，在真实特征上评估由合成集诱导的分类器，使分类器列向量充当特征空间中的类锚点；优化合成图像以最小化该判别损失。

Result: 在ImageNet-100上配四种预训练骨干，CLP-DD显著优于不带DSA的LGM，且以更低计算接近带DSA的LGM表现；在ImageNet-1K上，CLP-DD于四个骨干中的三个匹配或超过LGM+DSA，同时约14倍更快、显存占用小于1/8。

Conclusion: 在冻结特征+线性探针场景下，利用闭式解的内层求解并配合判别性外层目标至关重要；CLP-DD在精度-效率-内存上取得优越折中，减少了轨迹展开和NTK近似的需求。

Abstract: Dataset distillation compresses a large training set into a small synthetic set that preserves downstream training utility. While most existing methods target training networks from scratch, modern visual transfer learning often uses frozen pre-trained encoders followed by lightweight linear probing. Existing distillation methods for this setting either unroll iterative linear-probe updates with trajectory-based gradient matching, or rely on closed-form formulations originally designed for from-scratch training with neural-tangent-kernel (NTK) approximations. Neither route exploits the fact that frozen-feature linear probing admits a closed-form solution determined directly by the pre-trained features themselves, with no infinite-width approximation and no inner-loop trajectory. We propose Closed-Form Linear-Probe Dataset Distillation (CLP-DD), a bilevel formulation that computes the linear probe induced by the synthetic set with a sample-space kernel ridge solver. The synthetic images are then updated by evaluating this induced classifier on real features through a temperature-scaled softmax cross-entropy, where the classifier columns act as learned class anchors in feature space. We further show that the choice of outer objective is decisive: pairing the closed-form inner solver with a standard MSE outer loss substantially underperforms trajectory-based methods, while the discriminative outer loss closes most of the gap. On ImageNet-100 with four pre-trained backbones, CLP-DD substantially improves over LGM without DSA and approaches LGM with DSA at a fraction of the computational cost. On ImageNet-1K, CLP-DD matches or surpasses LGM with DSA on three of four backbones while running roughly $14\times$ faster and using less than one-eighth of the GPU memory.

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出ForeSight：以世界模型为核心的“先想象后决策”端到端自动驾驶规划框架，通过生成未来场景再做动作规划，显著优于现有反应式方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 两阶段：1) 利用预训练世界模型生成多种可行的未来视觉场景；2) 在这些想象的未来上进行条件规划，输出动作。世界模型不再是辅助，而是驱动动作预测的主体。

Result: 在NAVSIM与nuScenes上，显式未来想象带来显著性能提升，超过先前SOTA端到端规划方法。
